1. SSH into perlmutter, check default modules.
```
ml
Currently Loaded Modules:
  1) craype-x86-milan     4) xpmem/2.6.2-2.5_2.38__gd067c3f.shasta   7) cray-libsci/23.12.5  10) gcc-native/12.3         13) cudatoolkit/12.2
  2) libfabric/1.15.2.0   5) PrgEnv-gnu/8.5.0                        8) cray-mpich/8.1.28    11) perftools-base/23.12.0  14) craype-accel-nvidia80
  3) craype-network-ofi   6) cray-dsmml/0.2.2                        9) craype/2.7.30        12) cpe/23.12               15) gpu/1.0

```
2. Create a module script needed for the compilation and run it.
```
vi perl_env.sh
    module load cray-hdf5
    module load cray-netcdf
    module load openmpi

source perl_env.sh

ml
Currently Loaded Modules:
  1) craype-x86-milan     4) xpmem/2.6.2-2.5_2.38__gd067c3f.shasta   7) craype/2.7.30           10) cpe/23.12              13) gpu/1.0                   16) openmpi/5.0.3 (mpi)
  2) libfabric/1.15.2.0   5) PrgEnv-gnu/8.5.0                        8) gcc-native/12.3         11) cudatoolkit/12.2       14) cray-hdf5/1.12.2.9  (io)
  3) craype-network-ofi   6) cray-dsmml/0.2.2                        9) perftools-base/23.12.0  12) craype-accel-nvidia80  15) cray-netcdf/4.9.0.9 (io)

  Where:
   mpi:  MPI Providers
   io:   Input/output software
```
3. Clone COAWST in your home repo.
```
git clone --recursive -j8 https://github.com/DOI-USGS/COAWST.git
cd COAWST
```
4. We are going to do the Estuary_test2 example. Put ```build_roms.py``` in ```Projects/Estuary_test2```.
5. To run the script with the default settings, which is ROMS-only for this example, which compiles with ```gfortran```, we need to edit ```COAWST/Compilers/Linux-gfortran.mk```. Delete the components that reference the coupler information. Some of the ```nf-config``` and ```netcdf``` paths need to be manually set because ```--flibs``` is deprecated on the machine. If you skip either step, the build script will fail. Note that the changes to the ```nf-config``` and ```netcdf``` paths will need to updated in time if perlmutter depecates them, but they should be ok for a few years at least (from 2024). 
```
vi Linux-gfortran.mk

#Delete this 
ifndef USE_SCRIP
             LIBS += $(MCT_PARAMS_DIR)/mct_coupler_params.o
             LIBS += $(MCT_PARAMS_DIR)/mod_coupler_iounits.o
             LIBS += $(MCT_PARAMS_DIR)/get_sparse_matrix.o
endif

#Delete this 
ifdef USE_MCT
       MCT_INCDIR ?= /usr/local/mct/include
       MCT_LIBDIR ?= /usr/local/mct/lib
           FFLAGS += -I$(MCT_INCDIR)
             LIBS += -L$(MCT_LIBDIR) -lmct -lmpeu
           INCDIR += $(MCT_INCDIR) $(INCDIR)
endif

#Modify the code below
ifdef USE_NETCDF4
        NF_CONFIG ?= nf-config
    NETCDF_INCDIR ?= $(shell $(NF_CONFIG) --prefix)/include
             LIBS += $(shell $(NF_CONFIG) --flibs)
           INCDIR += $(NETCDF_INCDIR) $(INCDIR)

#To this
ifdef USE_NETCDF4
        NF_CONFIG ?= nf-config
    NETCDF_INCDIR ?= /opt/cray/pe/netcdf/4.9.0.3/gnu/9.1/include
             LIBS += -L/opt/cray/pe/netcdf/4.9.0.3/gnu/9.1/lib -lnetcdf -lnetcdff
           INCDIR += $(NETCDF_INCDIR) $(INCDIR)
else
```
6. Run the build script. Example output from a previous run is shown.
```
python build-roms.py --clean estuary_test2

Removing Build directory...
ROMS_APPLICATION=ESTUARY_TEST2
FORT=gfortran
USE_MPI=
USE_MPIF90=
USE_NETCDF4=on
USE_DEBUG=
USE_LARGE=on
MY_HEADER_DIR=/global/u2/d/dylan617/COAWST/Projects/Estuary_test2
MY_ANALYTICAL_DIR=/global/u2/d/dylan617/COAWST/Projects/Estuary_test2/Functionals
BINDIR=/global/u2/d/dylan617/COAWST/Projects/Estuary_test2
SCRATCH_DIR=/global/u2/d/dylan617/COAWST/Projects/Estuary_test2/Build
$gitrev is cbc5300fca6dffd9e954961637ceef6d35bd039d

cp -f /opt/cray/pe/netcdf/4.9.0.3/gnu/9.1/include/typesizes.mod /global/u2/d/dylan617/COAWST/Projects/Estuary_test2/Build
cp -p /global/homes/d/dylan617/make_macros.mk /global/u2/d/dylan617/COAWST/Projects/Estuary_test2/Build

```
7. If the compilation is successful, it will produce the executable file ```coawstS```.
8. Run COAWST in serial as shown below. Sample output is also shown.
```
./coawstS < ./ocean_estuary_test2.in

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 Model Input Parameters:  ROMS/TOMS version 4.1  
                          Friday - July 12, 2024 - 11:20:38 AM
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 Suspended Sediment Test in an Estuary

 Physical Parameters, Grid: 01
 =============================

      43200  ntimes            Number of timesteps for 3-D equations.
     10.000  dt                Timestep size (s) for 3-D equations.
         20  ndtfast           Number of timesteps for 2-D equations between
                                 each 3D timestep.
          1  ERstr             Starting ensemble/perturbation run number.
          1  ERend             Ending ensemble/perturbation run number.
          0  nrrec             Number of restart records to read from disk.
          T  LcycleRST         Switch to recycle time-records in restart file.
        720  nRST              Number of timesteps between the writing of data
                                 into restart fields.
         10  ninfo             Number of timesteps between print of information
                                 to standard output.
          T  ldefout           Switch to create a new output NetCDF file(s).
        360  nHIS              Number of timesteps between the writing fields
                                 into history file.
          0  nQCK              Number of timesteps between the writing fields
                                 into quicksave file.
 1.0000E-03  nl_visc2          NLM Horizontal, harmonic mixing coefficient
                                 (m2/s) for momentum.
          F  LuvSponge         Turning OFF sponge on horizontal momentum.
          F  LtracerSponge(01) Turning OFF sponge on tracer 01: temp
          F  LtracerSponge(02) Turning OFF sponge on tracer 02: salt
 5.0000E-06  Akt_bak(01)       Background vertical mixing coefficient (m2/s)
                                 for tracer 01: temp
 5.0000E-06  Akt_bak(02)       Background vertical mixing coefficient (m2/s)
                                 for tracer 02: salt
 5.0000E-05  Akv_bak           Background vertical mixing coefficient (m2/s)
                                 for momentum.
 5.0000E-06  Akk_bak           Background vertical mixing coefficient (m2/s)
                                 for turbulent energy.
 5.0000E-06  Akp_bak           Background vertical mixing coefficient (m2/s)
                                 for turbulent generic statistical field.
      3.000  gls_p             GLS stability exponent.
      1.500  gls_m             GLS turbulent kinetic energy exponent.
     -1.000  gls_n             GLS turbulent length scale exponent.
```
